msg:We stayed in two parts of the hotel; the single-storey villa and in the suite. 

It‚Äôs important to know that the villa is not in the same place as the hotel, and you do not have access to the facilities, including the restaurant and bar. The villa is 30 minutes walk from the hotel but you do have access to a golf cart driver. 

We did not know this when we booked, so we only stayed in the villa for one night, then moved to the main hotel for the second night. 

I would like to give special mention to two people; Mr Sky Yang and Ms Tiffany. These two people made our trip extra special. 
Firstly, Mr Sky made sure that a vehicle was always available to us. He went above and beyond to make sure we had a great experience; collecting us from the car park and driving us around the site. He was always prompt, punctual and courteous and we are extremely grateful for all his hard work. 

Secondly, Tiffany in reservations helped us fix the problem when we needed to change our reservation to move to the hotel so that we could rejoin our friends. She went above and beyond in every way, even answering my messages on her day off (we didn‚Äôt realise she was not at work). Tiffany helped resolve a tricky situation and made sure our holiday was saved and that we were able to rejoin our friends. 

Huge thanks to Mr Sky and Ms Tiffany! 

Regarding the villa, it is beautiful, clean and very private. The only negative is that you are a long way from everything else. You can use the very effective driver service but it‚Äôs important to know what to expect, that you are not near to the other facilities, and all good and drink is via room service. 

The bedroom, living room and dressing room are well equipped, and we loved the steam room and sauna within the bathroom. An unexpected bonus! 

The inside tub and outside pool are both very large and spacious. They fill very quickly and the water temperature is customisable to your tastes. 

I would definitely return to the villa another time for a romantic break. 

The castle is very different! The rooms are themed based on the tower. We stayed in the Glacier tower. I loved the turquoise and polar bear theme! The hotel is very child-friendly and lots of fun. The decor is very colourful and beautiful with lots of comfy chairs to sit on in the public spaces. 

The bed was very comfortable and the suite was lovely. 

I would stay in both these locations again. Hopefully this review can help you choose which is the right place for you!

msg:I was particularly moved at Haihua Island Bay. The only difference between here and Disney is the "princess üë∏". The beauty here is distorted, but it needs more IP and content to stimulate the space for commercial value.

The castles, hotels, entertainment facilities, catering, shopping, and services here are not inferior to those of Disneyland Paris and Europa.

It is a kind of great and lonely sense of desolation, which is shrouded in the regret of the past glory, but also mixed with a bit of regret that the present is different from the past.

But has it really been "different from the past"?

Maybe it's the best at this time. There is no need to queue up in the scorching sun. There are special cars to pick up and drop off every water project. You can go to play more projects at any time. An ice cream in the park is 20 yuan, and a cup of coconut milk is 25 yuan. The cost performance is sincere enough. Although not all projects are open all day at any time, the arrangements are also very reasonable. Basically, you can play them all in order. Little treasures can also have fun. Adults are even more excited. I played in the water world for a whole day and an afternoon, which was super exciting. We watched various cute animal performances in the Ocean World according to the schedule. I cried a lot when I watched the white whale performance. It was very amazing. Before watching the dolphin performance, the big screen repeatedly played news events about people rescuing dolphins, which earned me another wave of tears. The harmony between man and nature and the underlying thinking of animal protection are all taken care of. The arrangement of these details and the output of values ‚Äã‚Äãcan make the travel more meaningful.

It is particularly worth mentioning that the service. I often refuse to answer strange calls, but after booking the European Castle, I picked up Zhenyu's call from the European Castle Hotel. The next step is to start a full-time caring butler journey. Zhenyu's information is very timely, and the itinerary recommended for us is also very reasonable.

The three-day and two-night trip to Haihua Island was very happy. The hotel is super beautiful! The breakfast is very rich! The dinner is also very good! It is a good choice for family travel! It really won't step on the pit! You can come to play decisively. It's worry-free and super value. In addition, when you come to Haihua Island, you can really understand the greatness of the infrastructure of a big country!

Our Haihua Island should not be inferior to Disneyland Paris and Europa at all. I hope Ocean Flower Island will be better. üå∫

After reporting it to the housekeeper, waiters and engineers will soon come to repair it. The sanitation was also very clean. Breakfast is okay, but you get the bracelets after 12 noon every day. Choosing to stay at this hotel is more convenient for tourists who land on the island. The standard room of this luxury hotel with more than 5,001 rooms is only 304 yuan per night. Who wouldn't choose it at such a cost-effective price. They also specially sent a staff member Fu Zhuangshen to guide us, which is really considerate service. The sea view room I stayed in with two breakfasts was only 423 yuan a night, and the buffet breakfast was quite good, and the value was 128 yuan. Only the occupancy rate seems to be very low. The hotel is divided into four areas: Glacier Castle, Desert Castle, Ocean Castle, and Forest Castle. It seems that only the first two castles are open, and the latter two have almost no guests. The lobby is super luxurious, and the square in front of the door is also built in European style. I really hope this hotel will one day be hard to come by.

This time we are The two good friends brought the children here, because it was in time for the holidays and there were indeed more people. The hotel parking lot is no longer available. You have to take a bus from the P3 parking lot on Island 3 to the hotel. Although it is usually very convenient, However, there are many people and loopholes in management. The experience of entering the island is not very good. After arriving at the hotel, you can check in by yourself, which is very convenient. We were lucky. When we checked in, we happened to meet the lobby manager Lin Jiahua , He was very attentive and patient to help us, let us clean up the unpleasantness before, take the scenic train all the way to the food street in the evening, all kinds of food are dazzling, and enjoy the scenery along the way after the meal, it is really pleasant! However, after watching the light show and preparing to take the small train back to the hotel, it is not so beautiful. Because there are many people and few cars, fortunately, we left the phone number of the lobby manager Lin Jiahua. After the communication, he quickly contacted the concierge depar**ent and gave I was so happy to have a bus to pick us up. For this trip, I would like to thank Aalborg Hotel for having such an excellent lobby manager. Both in terms of business and service, I would like to praise him. At the same time, I also hope that the hotel can improve as soon as possible on some shortcomings. I hope the hotel will become better and better! May Hainan get better and better!
